<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследник.html>насле́дник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naslédnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследник.html>насле́дника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследник.html>насле́дники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследник.html>насле́дников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследница.html>насле́дница</a></b>)

***наследование.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наследование.html>насле́дование</a> (25926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследовать.html>насле́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naslédovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследование.html>насле́дование</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naslédovanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследование.html>насле́дования</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследование.html>насле́дования</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наследование.html>насле́дований</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inheritance, inheriting</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насмерть.html>на́смерть</a> (8145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насмерть.html>на́смерть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">násmertʹ</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шка</a> (6089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasméška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шек</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a> (11899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasós</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pump
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водяной.html>водяно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodjanój <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">water pump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручка.html>ру́чка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́са</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rúčka <b>nasósa</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pump handle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питательный.html>пита́тельный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pitátelʹnyj <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">feed pump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">нагнета́тельный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nagnetátelʹnyj <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">force pump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожарный.html>пожа́рный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">požárnyj <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fire pump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:центробежный.html>центробе́жный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">centrobéžnyj <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">rotary pump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">циркуляцио́нный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cirkuljaciónnyj <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">circulation pump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывать.html>вса́сывающий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsásyvajuščij <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">suction pump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">грязево́й <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насос.html>насо́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grjazevój <b>nasós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sludge pump, mud pump, sludger</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***наст.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a> (12528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, formed as if from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*настъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*nastŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="Cyrs" lang="orv">*стъ</span>, combining form of the Proto-Indo-European root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">обнастывати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnastyvati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рознастити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">roznastiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to uncover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nast</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>на́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>на́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>на́стов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>solid crust formed on snow after thawing and refreezing</li></ol>

***наставить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наставить.html>наста́вить</a> (13150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставить.html>наста́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставлять.html>наставля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put, to place, to set <i>(many)</i></li>
<li>to piece (on), to add, to add a piece, to put on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставить.html>наста́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рога́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nastávitʹ rogá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cuckold.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lengthen</li>
<li>to aim, to level, to point</li>
<li>to instruct, to admonish, to edify, to exhort</li>
<li>to teach</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставник.html>наста́вник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nastávnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***наставление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наставление.html>наставле́ние</a> (12968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставить.html>наста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставление.html>наставле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastavlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставление.html>наставле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставление.html>наставле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставление.html>наставле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>directions, instructions</li>
<li>admonition, precept, exhortation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наставление.html>наставле́ние</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délatʹ <b>nastavlénije</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">exhort;admonish;give a talking-to</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> manual</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наставлять.html>наставля́ть</a> (14149)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставить.html>наста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставлять.html>наставля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставить.html>наста́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put, to place, to set <i>(many)</i></li>
<li>to piece (on), to add, to add a piece, to put on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставлять.html>наставля́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рога</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nastavljátʹ roga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cuckold.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lengthen</li>
<li>to aim, to level, to point</li>
<li>to instruct, to admonish, to edify, to exhort</li>
<li>to teach</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наставляющий.html>наставля́ющий</a> (14149)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наставляющий.html>наставля́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastavljájuščij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настаивать.html>наста́ивать</a> (3381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настаивать.html>наста́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastáivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настоять.html>настоя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to insist, to persist, to press on, to put one's foot down</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настаивать.html>наста́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastáivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настоять.html>настоя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw, to extract, to infuse</li></ol>

***настать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настать.html>наста́ть</a> (4714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">statʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настать.html>наста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">настава́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to come, to begin (of time)
